aria-label="Breadcrumbs"><ul class="breadcrumbs"><li class="breadcrumbs__item"><a class="breadcrumbs__link" href="/weaviate/manage-collections"><span>How-to: Manage collections</span></a></li><li tocMobile_ITEo"><button type="button" class="clean-btn tocCollapsibleButton_TO0P">On this page</button></div><div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><header><h1>Vectorizer and vector index config</h1></header><div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-info admonition_xJq3 alert alert--info"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 2.3c3.14 0 5.7 2.56 5.7 5.7s-2.56 5.7-5.7 5.7A5.71 5.71 0 0 1 1.3 8c0-3.14 2.56-5.7 5.7-5.7zM7 1C3.14 1 0 4.14 0 8s3.14 7 7 7 7-3.14 7-7-3.14-7-7-7zm1 3H6v5h2V4zm0 6H6v2h2v-2z"></path></svg></span>Python and JS/TS client - Vectorizer Configuration API Changes</div><div class="admonitionContent_BuS1"><p>Starting with Weaviate Python client <code>v4.16.0</code>, the <a class="" href="/weaviate/client-libraries/python#vectorizer-api-changes-v4160">vectorizer configuration API has been updated</a>.<br>
<!-- -->Starting with Weaviate JS/TS client <code>v3.8.0</code>, the <a class="" href="/weaviate/client-libraries/typescript#vectorizer-api-changes-v380">vectorizer configuration API has been updated</a>.</p><p>Action required: <strong>Update to the latest client version</strong> and migrate your code to use the <a class="" href="/weaviate/manage-collections/vector-config#specify-a-vectorizer">new vectorizer configuration API</a>.</p></div></div>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="specify-a-vectorizer">Specify a vectorizer<a href="#specify-a-vectorizer" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Specify a vectorizer" title="Direct link to Specify a vectorizer" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<p>Specify a <code>vectorizer</code> for a collection.</p>
<details class="details_lb9f alert alert--info details_b_Ee" data-collapsed="true"><summary>Additional information</summary><div><div class="collapsibleContent_i85q"><p>Collection level settings override default values and general configuration parameters such as <a class="" href="/deploy/configuration/env-vars">environment variables</a>.</p><ul>
<li class=""><a class="" href="/weaviate/model-providers">Available model integrations</a></li>
<li class=""><a class="" href="/weaviate/config-refs/collections#vector-configuration">Vectorizer configuration references</a></li>
</ul></div></div></details>

<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="specify-vectorizer-settings">Specify vectorizer settings<a href="#specify-vectorizer-settings" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Specify vectorizer settings" title="Direct link to Specify vectorizer settings" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<!-- -->
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-caution admonition_xJq3 alert alert--warning"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 16 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M8.893 1.5c-.183-.31-.52-.5-.887-.5s-.703.19-.886.5L.138 13.499a.98.98 0 0 0 0 1.001c.193.31.53.501.886.501h13.964c.367 0 .704-.19.877-.5a1.03 1.03 0 0 0 .01-1.002L8.893 1.5zm.133 11.497H6.987v-2.003h2.039v2.003zm0-3.004H6.987V5.987h2.039v4.006z"></path></svg></span>.Vectors.text2vec_xxx with AutoSchema</div><div class="admonitionContent_BuS1"><p>Defining a collection with <code>Configure.Vectors.text2vec_xxx()</code> with Python client library <code>4.16.0</code>-<code>4.16.3</code> will throw an error if no properties are defined and <code>vectorize_collection_name</code> is not set to <code>True</code>.</p><p>This is addressed in <code>4.16.4</code> of the Weaviate Python client. See this FAQ entry for more details: <a class="" href="/weaviate/more-resources/faq#q-invalid-properties-error-when-creating-a-collection-python-client-versions-4160-to-4163">Invalid properties error in Python client versions 4.16.0 to 4.16.3</a>.</p></div></div>
<p>To configure how a vectorizer works (i.e. what model to use) with a specific collection, set the vectorizer parameters.</p>

<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="define-named-vectors">Define named vectors<a href="#define-named-vectors" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Define named vectors" title="Direct link to Define named vectors" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-info admonition_xJq3 alert alert--info"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 2.3c3.14 0 5.7 2.56 5.7 5.7s-2.56 5.7-5.7 5.7A5.71 5.71 0 0 1 1.3 8c0-3.14 2.56-5.7 5.7-5.7zM7 1C3.14 1 0 4.14 0 8s3.14 7 7 7 7-3.14 7-7-3.14-7-7-7zm1 3H6v5h2V4zm0 6H6v2h2v-2z"></path></svg></span>Added in <code>v1.24</code></div></div>
<p>You can define multiple <a class="" href="/weaviate/concepts/data#multiple-vector-embeddings-named-vectors">named vectors</a> per collection. This allows each object to be represented by multiple vector embeddings, each with its own vector index.</p>
<p>As such, each named vector configuration can include its own vectorizer and vector index settings.</p>
<div class="codeDropdownContainer_uCK5 code"><div class="codeDropdownHeader_PNgx"><div class="leftSection_ieqF"><span class="languageLabel_LeYV"></span><div class="languageSelector_Mp0Y"><select class="languageDropdown_BTMK"><option value="py" selected="">Python</option><option value="ts">JavaScript/TypeScript</option><option value="go">Go</option><option value="java6">Java v6</option><option value="java">Java v5 (Deprecated)</option><option value="csharp">C# (Beta)</option></select><img src="/img/site/logo-py.svg" alt="" class="languageIcon_e8S9"><svg class="dropdownArrow_T7wX" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M5.293 7.293a1 1 0 011.414 0L10 10.586l3.293-3.293a1 1 0 111.414 1.414l-4 4a1 1 0 01-1.414 0l-4-4a1 1 0 010-1.414z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg></div></div><div class="rightSection__3jI"><a href="https://weaviate-python-client.readthedocs.io/en/stable" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="apiDocsLink_EDfG" title="View API documentation"><img src="/img/site/logo-py.svg" alt="py docs" height="12" width="12" style="vertical-align:middle"><span style="vertical-align:middle">  API docs</span></a><div class="versionInfo_e5Um"><span class="versionLabel_YSKW">More info<span class="tooltip_vwsi"><svg width="11" height="11" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor" class="infoIcon_bJII"><path d="M12 2C6.48 2 2 6.48 2 12s4.48 10 10 10 10-4.48 10-10S17.52 2 12 2zm1 15h-2v-6h2v6zm0-8h-2V7h2v2z"></path></svg><span class="tooltipContent_QizM" data-position="left">Code snippets in the documentation reflect the latest client library and Weaviate Database version. class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">[</span><span <h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="add-new-named-vectors">Add new named vectors<a href="#add-new-named-vectors" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Add new named vectors" title="Direct link to Add new named vectors" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-info admonition_xJq3 alert alert--info"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 2.3c3.14 0 5.7 2.56 5.7 5.7s-2.56 5.7-5.7 5.7A5.71 5.71 0 0 1 1.3 8c0-3.14 2.56-5.7 5.7-5.7zM7 1C3.14 1 0 4.14 0 8s3.14 7 7 7 7-3.14 7-7-3.14-7-7-7zm1 3H6v5h2V4zm0 6H6v2h2v-2z"></path></svg></span>Added in <code>v1.31</code></div></div>
<p>Named vectors can be added to existing collection definitions with named vectors. (This is not possible for collections without named vectors.)</p>
<div class="codeDropdownContainer_uCK5 code"><div class="codeDropdownHeader_PNgx"><div class="leftSection_ieqF"><span class="languageLabel_LeYV"></span><div class="languageSelector_Mp0Y"><select class="languageDropdown_BTMK"><option value="py" selected="">Python</option><option value="ts">JavaScript/TypeScript</option><option value="go">Go</option><option value="java6">Java v6</option><option value="csharp">C# (Beta)</option></select><img src="/img/site/logo-py.svg" alt="" class="languageIcon_e8S9"><svg class="dropdownArrow_T7wX" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M5.293 7.293a1 1 0 011.414 0L10 10.586l3.293-3.293a1 1 0 111.414 1.414l-4 4a1 1 0 01-1.414 0l-4-4a1 1 0 010-1.414z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg></div></div><div class="rightSection__3jI"><a href="https://weaviate-python-client.readthedocs.io/en/stable" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="apiDocsLink_EDfG" title="View API documentation"><img src="/img/site/logo-py.svg" alt="py docs" height="12" width="12" style="vertical-align:middle"><span style="vertical-align:middle">  API docs</span></a><div class="versionInfo_e5Um"><span class="versionLabel_YSKW">More info<span class="tooltip_vwsi"><svg width="11" height="11" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor" class="infoIcon_bJII"><path d="M12 2C6.48 2 2 6.48 2 12s4.48 10 10 10 10-4.48 10-10S17.52 2 12 2zm1 15h-2v-6h2v6zm0-8h-2V7h2v2z"></path></svg><span class="tooltipContent_QizM" data-position="left">Code snippets in the documentation reflect the latest client library and Weaviate Database version. <div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-caution admonition_xJq3 alert alert--warning"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 16 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M8.893 1.5c-.183-.31-.52-.5-.887-.5s-.703.19-.886.5L.138 13.499a.98.98 0 0 0 0 1.001c.193.31.53.501.886.501h13.964c.367 0 .704-.19.877-.5a1.03 1.03 0 0 0 .01-1.002L8.893 1.5zm.133 11.497H6.987v-2.003h2.039v2.003zm0-3.004H6.987V5.987h2.039v4.006z"></path></svg></span>Objects aren&#x27;t automatically revectorized</div><div class="admonitionContent_BuS1"><p>Adding a new vector to the collection definition <a class="" href="/weaviate/concepts/data#adding-a-named-vector-after-collection-creation">won&#x27;t trigger vectorization for existing objects</a>. Only objects created after the vector addition will receive these new vector embeddings.</p></div></div>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="define-multi-vector-embeddings-eg-colbert-colpali">Define multi-vector embeddings (e.g. ColBERT, ColPali)<a href="#define-multi-vector-embeddings-eg-colbert-colpali" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Define multi-vector embeddings (e.g. ColBERT, ColPali)" title="Direct link to Define multi-vector embeddings (e.g. ColBERT, ColPali)" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-info admonition_xJq3 alert alert--info"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 2.3c3.14 0 5.7 2.56 5.7 5.7s-2.56 5.7-5.7 5.7A5.71 5.71 0 0 1 1.3 8c0-3.14 2.56-5.7 5.7-5.7zM7 1C3.14 1 0 4.14 0 8s3.14 7 7 7 7-3.14 7-7-3.14-7-7-7zm1 3H6v5h2V4zm0 6H6v2h2v-2z"></path></svg></span>Added in <code>v1.29</code>, <code>v1.30</code></div></div>
<p>Multi-vector embeddings, also known as multi-vectors, represent a single object with multiple vectors, i.e. a 2-dimensional matrix. Multi-vectors are currently only available for HNSW indexes for named vectors. To use multi-vectors, enable it for the appropriate named vector.</p>
<div class="codeDropdownContainer_uCK5 code"><div class="codeDropdownHeader_PNgx"><div class="leftSection_ieqF"><span class="languageLabel_LeYV"></span><div class="languageSelector_Mp0Y"><select class="languageDropdown_BTMK"><option value="py" selected="">Python</option><option value="ts">JavaScript/TypeScript</option><option value="java6">Java v6</option><option value="java">Java v5 (Deprecated)</option><option value="csharp">C# (Beta)</option></select><img src="/img/site/logo-py.svg" alt="" class="languageIcon_e8S9"><svg class="dropdownArrow_T7wX" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M5.293 7.293a1 1 0 011.414 0L10 10.586l3.293-3.293a1 1 0 111.414 1.414l-4 4a1 1 0 01-1.414 0l-4-4a1 1 0 010-1.414z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg></div></div><div class="rightSection__3jI"><a href="https://weaviate-python-client.readthedocs.io/en/stable" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="apiDocsLink_EDfG" title="View API documentation"><img src="/img/site/logo-py.svg" alt="py docs" height="12" width="12" style="vertical-align:middle"><span style="vertical-align:middle">  API docs</span></a><div class="versionInfo_e5Um"><span class="versionLabel_YSKW">More info<span class="tooltip_vwsi"><svg width="11" height="11" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor" class="infoIcon_bJII"><path d="M12 2C6.48 2 2 6.48 2 12s4.48 10 10 10 10-4.48 10-10S17.52 2 12 2zm1 15h-2v-6h2v6zm0-8h-2V7h2v2z"></path></svg><span class="tooltipContent_QizM" data-position="left">Code snippets in the documentation reflect the latest client library and Weaviate Database version. Check the<!-- --> <a href="/weaviate/release-notes">Release notes</a> <!-- -->for specific versions.<br><br>If a snippet doesn&#x27;t work or you have feedback, please open a<!-- --> <a href="https://github.com/weaviate/docs/issues/new?template=doc_feedback.yml&amp;title=%5BDocumentation+Feedback%5D%3A+&amp;labels=user-feedback&amp;page-url=" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">GitHub issue</a>.</span></span></span></div></div></div><div class="codeContent_E0WP"><div class="tabPanel_nEcw" style="display:block" aria-hidden="false"><div role="tabpanel" class="tabItem_Ymn6"><div><div class="language-py codeBlockContainer_Ckt0 theme-code-block" style="--prism-color:#393A34;--prism-background-color:#f6f8fa"><div class="codeBlockContent_QJqH"><pre class-name">Property</span><span class="token attribute class-name punctuation" style="color:#393A34">.</span><span class="token attribute class-name">Text</span><span class="token attribute attribute-arguments punctuation" style="color:#393A34">(</span><span class="token attribute attribute-arguments string" style="color:#e3116c">&quot;text&quot;</span><span class="token attribute attribute-arguments punctuation" style="color:#393A34">)</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">]</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">,</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">}</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">)</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:#393A34">;</span><span class="token plain"></span><br></span><span class="token-line" style="color:#393A34"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token comment" style="color:#999988;font-style:italic">// Coming soon</span><br></span></code></pre></div></div><div class="flex flex-wrap gap-2 mt-2"></div></div></div></div></div></div>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-tip admonition_xJq3 alert alert--success"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 12 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M6.5 0C3.48 0 1 2.19 1 5c0 .92.55 2.25 1 3 1.34 2.25 1.78 2.78 2 4v1h5v-1c.22-1.22.66-1.75 2-4 .45-.75 1-2.08 1-3 0-2.81-2.48-5-5.5-5zm3.64 7.48c-.25.44-.47.8-.67 1.11-.86 1.41-1.25 2.06-1.45 3.23-.02.05-.02.11-.02.17H5c0-.06 0-.13-.02-.17-.2-1.17-.59-1.83-1.45-3.23-.2-.31-.42-.67-.67-1.11C2.44 6.78 2 5.65 2 5c0-2.2 2.02-4 4.5-4 1.22 0 2.36.42 3.22 1.19C10.55 2.94 11 3.94 11 5c0 .66-.44 1.78-.86 2.48zM4 14h5c-.23 1.14-1.3 2-2.5 2s-2.27-.86-2.5-2z"></path></svg></span>Use quantization and encoding to compress your vectors</div><div class="admonitionContent_BuS1"><p>Multi-vector embeddings use up more memory than single vector embeddings. You can use <a class="" href="/weaviate/configuration/compression">vector quantization</a> and <a class="" href="/weaviate/configuration/compression/multi-vectors#muvera-encoding">encoding</a> to compress them and reduce memory usage.</p></div></div>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="set-vector-index-type">Set vector index type<a href="#set-vector-index-type" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Set vector index type" title="Direct link to Set vector index type" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<p>The vector index type can be set for each collection at creation time, between <code>hnsw</code>, <code>flat</code> and <code>dynamic</code> index types.</p>

<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="set-vector-index-parameters">Set vector index parameters<a href="#set-vector-index-parameters" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Set vector index parameters" title="Direct link to Set vector index parameters" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<p>Set vector index parameters such as <a class="" href="/weaviate/configuration/compression">compression</a> and <a class="" href="/weaviate/concepts/filtering#filter-strategy">filter strategy</a> through collection configuration. Some parameters can be <a class="" href="/weaviate/manage-collections/collection-operations#update-a-collection-definition">updated later</a> after collection creation.</p>

<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="property-level-settings">Property-level settings<a href="#property-level-settings" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Property-level settings" title="Direct link to Property-level settings" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<p>Configure individual properties in a collection. Each property can have it&#x27;s own configuration. Here are some common settings:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">Vectorize the property</li>
<li class="">Vectorize the property name</li>
<li class="">Set a <a class="" href="/weaviate/config-refs/collections#tokenization">tokenization type</a></li>
</ul>

<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="specify-a-distance-metric">Specify a distance metric<a href="#specify-a-distance-metric" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Specify a distance metric" title="Direct link to Specify a distance metric" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<p>If you choose to bring your own vectors, you should specify the <code>distance metric</code>.</p>
